operations = {
	repair_baltic_fleet_desision = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_naval
		available = {
			controls_state = 195
			controls_state = 1372
		}
		
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = baltic_fleet_in_exile
			OR = {
				owns_state = 219
				AND = {
					is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
					OR = {
						controls_state = 195
						controls_state = 1372
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		cost = 50
		
		days_remove = 14
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = baltic_fleet_in_exile
			load_oob = RUS_1917_baltic_navy_legacy
		}
	}

russian_reunification_desisions = {
	national_assembly_desision = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		available = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly }
			219 = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
			NOT = { any_other_country = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus exists = yes } }
		}
		
		visible = {
			is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
			NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly }
			is_reactionary_country = yes
		}
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 219 = { OWNER = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } check_variable = { num_owned_states < 2 } } } }
				219 = { OWNER = { ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } } } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 219 } } transfer_state = 219 }
			add_state_core = 219
			set_capital = { state = 219 remember_old_capital = no }
			country_event = rcw_all_rus_NA.1
		}
	}
	second_constituent_assembly_desision = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		available = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly }
			219 = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
			NOT = { any_other_country = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus exists = yes } }
		}
		
		visible = {
			is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
			NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly }
			NOT = { is_reactionary_country = yes }
		}
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = RCW_national_assembly_replaced_by_second_constituent_assembly
			if = {
				limit = { 219 = { OWNER = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } check_variable = { num_owned_states < 2 } } } }
				219 = { OWNER = { ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } } } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 219 } } transfer_state = 219 }
			add_state_core = 219
			set_capital = { state = 219 remember_old_capital = no }

		}
	}
	second_civil_war_unify_russia_desision = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		available = {
			219 = { OWNER = { OR = { tag = ROOT is_subject_of = ROOT } } }
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
			NOT = { any_other_country = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus exists = yes } }
			NOT = { any_country = { exists = yes has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_revolt } }
			OR = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_member }
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_leader
				NOT = { any_other_country = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_leader exists = yes } }
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_loyal
					NOT = { any_other_country = { exists = yes has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_disloyal } }
				}
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_disloyal
					NOT = { any_other_country = { exists = yes has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_loyal } }
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { any_other_country = { exists = yes has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_disloyal } }
					NOT = { any_other_country = { exists = yes has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_loyal } }
				}
			}
			NOT = { any_other_country = { is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes exists = yes is_subject = no NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT } NOT = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_member has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_loyal has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_disloyal } NOT = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_peace_deal } } }
		}
		
		visible = {
			is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
			NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus }
			has_global_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly
		}
		
		cost = 0
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 219 = { OWNER = { NOT = { tag = ROOT } check_variable = { num_owned_states < 2 } } } }
				219 = { OWNER = { ROOT = { annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes } } } }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { NOT = { owns_state = 219 } } transfer_state = 219 }
			add_state_core = 219
			set_capital = { state = 219 remember_old_capital = no }
			country_event = rcw_all_rus_NA.23
		}
	}
	second_civil_war_separatist_leave_war_desision = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war
		available = {
			is_subject = no
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			any_enemy_country = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_former_russian_empire_russian_country_tt
					is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
				}
				has_idea = russia_in_ruins_idea
			}
			surrender_progress < 0.5
		}
		
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_focus_tree = Russia_Bolsheviks_focus }
			is_any_former_russian_empire_country = yes
			NOT = { is_main_former_russian_empire_country = yes }
			any_other_country = { is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes has_war_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_leader }
		}
		
		cost = 50
		
		days_remove = 60
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_all_rus_NA.25 hours = 1 }
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_former_russian_empire_russian_country = yes
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
				country_event = { id = rcw_all_rus_NA.26 hours = 1 }
			}
			country_event = { id = rcw_all_rus_NA.27 hours = 1 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								any_other_country = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_peace_deal }
								num_of_controlled_states > 10
							}
							any_other_country = {
								has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_peace_deal
								OR = {
									any_other_country = { has_country_flag = RCW_Allrussian_national_assembly_peace_deal }
									num_of_controlled_states > 10
								}
							}
							num_of_controlled_states > 20
						}
					}
					news_event = { id = news_n.28 days = 7 }
				}
				add_to_variable = { global.count_RUS_separatists = 1 }
				if = {
					limit = { num_of_controlled_states > 10 }
					add_to_variable = { global.count_RUS_separatists = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_5
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_4
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_3
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_2
				add_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { RUS_credit_pay = 0 } }
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_5
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_4
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_3
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_2
				remove_ideas = pay_Entente_credit_for_Russia_for_Russia_1
				clear_variable = RUS_credit_pay
			}
		}
	}

		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = UKR
				original_tag = RUS
			}
		}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_war_with = RUS
				has_war_with = UKR
			}
			AND = {
				UKR = {
					surrender_progress < 0.3
				}
				RUS = {
					surrender_progress > 0.2
				}
			}
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = RUS_civil_war_over }
			OR = {
				has_war_with = RUS
				has_war_with = UKR
			}
			UKR = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_directory_win
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = UKR_communist_peace_fired }
			is_subject = no
			RUS = { is_subject = no }
			UKR = { is_subject = no }
			FRT = { NOT = { is_subject_of = RUS } }
			GRG = { NOT = { is_subject_of = RUS } }
		}
		
		days_remove = 35
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = {
						tag = RUS
						surrender_progress > 0.2
						UKR = { surrender_progress < 0.1 }
					}
					AND = {
						tag = UKR
						RUS = { surrender_progress > 0.2 }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = POL_RUS_peace_delay
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = UKR }
				RUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine.59 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				UKR = { country_event = { id = ukraine.59 days = 1 } }
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			
		}
	}
